-- Migration: 20241204_oraculo_logs.sql

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS public.oraculo_logs (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  user_id UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  user_role TEXT NOT NULL,
  plan TEXT,
  url_atual TEXT,
  question TEXT NOT NULL,
  resposta_modo TEXT,
  resposta_risco TEXT,
  resposta_json JSONB,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
  flag_risco_alto BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE
);

-- Ãndices para performance
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_oraculo_logs_user_id ON public.oraculo_logs(user_id);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_oraculo_logs_risco ON public.oraculo_logs(resposta_risco);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_oraculo_logs_created_at ON public.oraculo_logs(created_at);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_oraculo_logs_flag_risco ON public.oraculo_logs(flag_risco_alto);

-- RLS
ALTER TABLE public.oraculo_logs ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

-- PolÃ­tica: admin pode ver todos os logs
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "admin_can_view_all_oraculo_logs" ON public.oraculo_logs;
CREATE POLICY "admin_can_view_all_oraculo_logs"
  ON public.oraculo_logs FOR SELECT
  USING (
    auth.uid() IN (
      SELECT id FROM auth.users 
      WHERE raw_user_meta_data->>'role' = 'admin'
    )
  );

-- PolÃ­tica: usuÃ¡rio pode ver seus prÃ³prios logs
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "user_can_view_own_oraculo_logs" ON public.oraculo_logs;
CREATE POLICY "user_can_view_own_oraculo_logs"
  ON public.oraculo_logs FOR SELECT
  USING (auth.uid() = user_id);

-- PolÃ­tica: qualquer usuÃ¡rio autenticado pode inserir
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "authenticated_can_insert_oraculo_logs" ON public.oraculo_logs;
CREATE POLICY "authenticated_can_insert_oraculo_logs"
  ON public.oraculo_logs FOR INSERT
  WITH CHECK (auth.uid() IS NOT NULL);

// app/api/oraculo-v2/route.ts

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
import { createClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server'

export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const supabase = await createClient()
    const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
    
    if (!user) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'NÃ£o autenticado' }, { status: 401 })
    }

    const body = await request.json()
    const { user_role, manual_context, language, url_atual, question, plan } = body

    if (!question) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Pergunta obrigatÃ³ria' }, { status: 400 })
    }

    // TODO: Chamar provedor de IA (OpenAI, Anthropic, etc.)
    // const aiResponse = await callOracleV2AI({
    //   user_role: user_role || 'usuaria',
    //   manual_context,
    //   language: language || 'pt-BR',
    //   url_atual,
    //   question,
    //   plan
    // })

    // Resposta mock para desenvolvimento
    const aiResponse = {
      modo: 'faq',
      risco: 'baixo',
      titulo_curto: 'Resposta do OrÃ¡culo',
      resposta_principal: 'Esta Ã© uma resposta de exemplo.',
      passos: [],
      links_sugeridos: [],
      mensagem_final_seguranÃ§a: ''
    }

    // Salvar log
    await supabase.from('oraculo_logs').insert({
      user_id: user.id,
      user_role: user_role || 'usuaria',
      plan,
      url_atual,
      question,
      resposta_modo: aiResponse.modo,
      resposta_risco: aiResponse.risco,
      resposta_json: aiResponse,
      flag_risco_alto: aiResponse.risco === 'alto'
    })

    return NextResponse.json(aiResponse)
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Erro no OrÃ¡culo V2:', error)
    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Erro interno' }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

=== ğŸ“‹ ESQUELETO: AskOracleButton.tsx ===

// components/AskOracleButton.tsx

'use client'

import { useState } from 'react'
import { MessageCircleQuestion, X, Send, Loader2 } from 'lucide-react'

interface OracleResponse {
  modo: string
  risco: string
  titulo_curto: string
  resposta_principal: string
  passos: string[]
  links_sugeridos: any[]
  mensagem_final_seguranÃ§a: string
}

export function AskOracleButton({ 
  userRole = 'usuaria',
  urlAtual = '',
  plan = 'free'
}: {
  userRole?: string
  urlAtual?: string
  plan?: string
}) {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false)
  const [question, setQuestion] = useState('')
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)
  const [response, setResponse] = useState<OracleResponse | null>(null)

  const handleSubmit = async () => {
    if (!question.trim()) return
    
    setLoading(true)
    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/oraculo-v2', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          user_role: userRole,
          language: 'pt-BR',
          url_atual: urlAtual || window.location.pathname,
          question,
          plan
        })
      })
      const data = await res.json()
      setResponse(data)
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Erro ao consultar OrÃ¡culo:', error)
    } finally {
      setLoading(false)
    }
  }

  return (
    <>
      {/* BotÃ£o flutuante */}
      <button
        onClick={() => setIsOpen(true)}
        className="fixed bottom-4 right-4 bg-purple-600 text-white p-4 rounded-full shadow-lg hover:bg-purple-700 z-50"
        title="Perguntar ao OrÃ¡culo"
      >
        <MessageCircleQuestion className="w-6 h-6" />
      </button>

      {/* Modal */}
      {isOpen && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/50 flex items-center justify-center z-50 p-4">
          <div className="bg-white rounded-lg max-w-lg w-full max-h-[80vh] overflow-hidden">
            {/* Header */}
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border-b">
              <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold flex items-center gap-2">
                <MessageCircleQuestion className="w-5 h-5 text-purple-600" />
                Perguntar ao OrÃ¡culo
              </h2>
              <button onClick={() => { setIsOpen(false); setResponse(null) }}>
                <X className="w-5 h-5" />
              </button>
            </div>

            {/* Content */}
            <div className="p-4 overflow-y-auto max-h-[60vh]">
              {!response ? (
                <div className="space-y-4">
                  <textarea
                    value={question}
                    onChange={(e) => setQuestion(e.target.value)}
                    placeholder="Digite sua dÃºvida..."
                    className="w-full p-3 border rounded-lg resize-none h-32"
                  />
                  <button
                    onClick={handleSubmit}
                    disabled={loading || !question.trim()}
                    className="w-full bg-purple-600 text-white py-2 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center gap-2 disabled:opacity-50"
                  >
                    {loading ? <Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin" /> : <Send className="w-4 h-4" />}
                    {loading ? 'Consultando...' : 'Enviar'}
                  </button>
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div className="space-y-4">
                  <h3 className="font-semibold">{response.titulo_curto}</h3>
                  <p className="text-gray-700">{response.resposta_principal}</p>
                  {response.passos.length > 0 && (
                    <ol className="list-decimal list-inside space-y-1">
                      {response.passos.map((passo, i) => (
                        <li key={i}>{passo}</li>
                      ))}
                    </ol>
                  )}
                  {response.mensagem_final_seguranÃ§a && (
                    <div className="bg-amber-50 border border-amber-200 p-3 rounded-lg text-sm">
                      {response.mensagem_final_seguranÃ§a}
                    </div>
                  )}
                  <button
                    onClick={() => { setResponse(null); setQuestion('') }}
                    className="w-full border py-2 rounded-lg"
                  >
                    Nova pergunta
                  </button>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </>
  )
}
